25:T4dc,You who believe, when you contract a debt for a stated term, put it down in writing: have a scribe write it down justly between you. No scribe should refuse to write: let him write as God has taught him, let the debtor dictate, and let him fear God, his Lord, and not diminish &#91;the debt&#93; at all. If the debtor is feeble-minded, weak, or unable to dictate, then let his guardian dictate justly. Call in two men as witnesses. If two men are not there, then call one man and two women out of those you approve as witnesses, so that if one of the two women should forget the other can remind her. Let the witnesses not refuse when they are summoned. Do not disdain to write the debt down, be it small or large, along with the time it falls due: this way is more equitable in God&rsquo;s eyes, more reliable as testimony, and more likely to prevent doubts arising between you. But if the merchandise is there and you hand it over, there is no blame on you if you do not write it down. Have witnesses present whenever you trade with one another, and let no harm be done to either scribe or witness, for if you did cause them harm, it would be a crime on your part. Be mindful of God, and He will teach you: He has full knowledge of everything26:T2012,<entryFree id="n13220" key="دَنَا" type="main">

[And <foreign lang="ar">أَدْنَى الفَمِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The fore,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">foremost, part of the mouth.</hi>] And <foreign lang="ar">الدُّنْيَا</foreign> [for <foreign lang="ar">الدَّارُ الدُّنْيَا</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">الحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">The former dwelling,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">abode,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">life;</hi> i. e. <hi rend="ital">the present world,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">life,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">state of existence</hi>]; <hi rend="ital">contr. of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الآخِرَةُ</foreign>: (M, K:) [or] it is so called because of its nearness: (T, S:) [and may be rendered <hi rend="ital">the sublunary abode,</hi> &amp;c.: and <hi rend="ital">the inferior abode,</hi> &amp;c. It also signifies <hi rend="ital">The enjoyments, blessings,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">good, of the present world,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">life; worldly blessings</hi> or <hi rend="ital">prosperity,</hi> &amp;c.] And sometimes it is with tenween, (K, TA,) when used indeterminately: (TA:) [thus,] IAar mentions the saying <foreign lang="ar">مَا لَهُ دُنْيًا وَ لَا آخِرَةٌ</foreign> [as meaning <hi rend="ital">He has none of the enjoyments,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">blessings, of the present world, nor</hi> in prospect <hi rend="ital">any enjoyments,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">blessings, of the world to come</hi>]; with tenween. (M, TA.) And you say, <foreign lang="ar">بَاعَ دُنْيَاهُ بِآخِرَتِهِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He purchased his enjoyments of the present world at the expense of his enjoyments of the world to come</hi>]. (Z, TA in art. <foreign lang="ar">بيع</foreign>.) And <foreign lang="ar">اَبْنُ الدُّنْيَا</foreign> means <hi rend="ital">The rich man.</hi> (Msb in art. <foreign lang="ar">بنى</foreign>.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">More,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">most, apt, fit,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proper:</hi> thus in the Kur [xxxiii. 59], in the phrase <foreign lang="ar">ذٰلِكَ أَدْنَى أَنْ يُعَرَفْنَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">That will be more,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">most, apt, fit,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proper, that they may be known</hi>]; (Ksh, Mgh;) i. e., that they may be known to be free women, as distinguished from female slaves, who did not cover their faces. (Jel.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">Less</hi> [<hi rend="ital">in number</hi> or <hi rend="ital">quantity</hi> &amp;c.], and <hi rend="ital">least</hi> [<hi rend="ital">therein</hi>]; opposed to <foreign lang="ar">أَكْثَرُ</foreign>. (TA.) <foreign lang="ar">وَلَا أَدْنَى مِنْ ذٰلِكَ وَلَاأَكْثَرَ</foreign>, in the Kur [lviii. 8], means <hi rend="ital">Nor less in number than that, nor more in number.</hi> (Bd.) And <foreign lang="ar">وَلَنُذِيقَنَّهُمْ مِنَ ٱلْعَذَابِ ٱلْأَدْنَى دُونَ ٱلْعَذَابِ ٱلْأَكْبَرِ</foreign>, in the Kur [xxxii. 21, lit. <hi rend="ital">And we will assuredly make them to taste of the smaller punishment besides the greater punishment</hi>], means, accord. to Zj, whatever punishment is inflicted in the present world and the punishment of the world to come. (M.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">Worse,</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">inferior</hi> in quality,] and <hi rend="ital">worst;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">more,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">most, low, ignoble, base, vile, mean,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">weak;</hi> opposed to <foreign lang="ar">خَيْرٌ</foreign>. (TA.) It is said in the Kur [ii. 58], <foreign lang="ar">أَتَسْتَبْدِلُونَ ٱلَّذِى هُوَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">أَدْنَى بِٱلَّذِى هُوَ خَيْرٌ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Will ye take in exchange that which is worse,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">inferior, for that which is better?</hi> or], accord. to Zj, meaning <hi rend="ital">that which is less in value</hi> [<hi rend="ital">for that which is better</hi>]? <foreign lang="ar">ادنى</foreign> being thus, without <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign>: Fr says that it is here from <foreign lang="ar">الدَّنَآءَةٌ</foreign>: and Zuheyr El-Kurkubee [or (accord. to some) El-Furkubee] read <foreign lang="ar">أَدْنَأُ</foreign>.
